<script>
	$(document).ready(function() {
		$('a[href*="https://up-t.jp/drawer/?session"]').each(function () {
			var href = $(this).attr('href').replace(/(session=)[^&]+/, '$1' + $('#tool_session').val());
			$(this).attr('data-link', href);
			$(this).removeAttr('href');
			$(this).attr('id', 'go_to_proc');
		});

		$('a[href*="/proc.php?run=go_to_drawtool"]').each(function () {
			var href = $(this).attr('href').replace('/proc.php?run=go_to_drawtool', 'https://up-t.jp/drawer?session=' + $('#tool_session').val());
			$(this).attr('data-link', href);
			$(this).removeAttr('href');
			$(this).attr('id', 'go_to_proc');
		});
	});

	$(document).on('click', '#go_to_proc', function(event) {
		event.preventDefault();
		var param = $(this).attr('data-link').split('?');
		var domain = param[0];
		var session = param[1];
		sessionStorage.setItem('DRAWPARAM', session);

        if(window.location.pathname == '/guide/howtoprint/foodprint'){
            var idItem = $(this).attr('data-item');
            sessionStorage.setItem('foodprint', idItem);
        }

		var expires = "";
		var date = new Date();
		date.setTime(date.getTime() + (15*60*60*1000));
		expires = "; expires=" + date.toUTCString();
		document.cookie = 'DRAWPARAM' + "=" + (session || "")  + expires + "; path=/";

		var target = $(this).attr('target');
		if (target === "_blank" || event.ctrlKey || event.metaKey) {
			window.open(domain, '_blank');
		} else {
			window.location.href = domain;
		}
	});

	$(document).on('click', '.btn-btn-new-color', function(event) {
		var image_id = $(this).attr('data-image-id');
		var cart_id = $(this).attr('data-cart-id');
		var tool_id = $(this).attr('data-tool');
		tool_id = (tool_id !== undefined) ? '&tool_id=' + tool_id : "";

		$.get('/proc.php?run=newColor&image_id=' + image_id +'&cart_id=' + cart_id + tool_id, function (response) {
			var param = response.split('?');
			var domain = param[0];
			var session = param[1];
			sessionStorage.setItem('DRAWPARAM', session);

			var expires = "";
			var date = new Date();
			date.setTime(date.getTime() + (15*60*60*1000));
			expires = "; expires=" + date.toUTCString();
			document.cookie = 'DRAWPARAM' + "=" + (session || "")  + expires + "; path=/";

			var target = $(this).attr('target');
			if (target === "_blank" || event.ctrlKey || event.metaKey) {
				window.open(domain, '_blank');
			} else {
				window.location.href = domain;
			}
		})
	})

	$(document).ready(function () {
        $(".search-common-input").keypress(function (e) {
            const btn = $(".pure-button-primary");

            if (e.which === 13) {
                $(".pure-button-primary").click();
                btn.prop('disabled', true);
            }
        })
	})
</script>
